    40 interface ModelContextValue {
    41   models: ModelConfig[];
    42   activeModel: ModelConfig | null;
    43   activeModelId: string;
    44   setActiveModelId: (id: string) => void;
    45   addModel: (model: Omit<ModelConfig, 'id'>) => void;
    46   updateModel: (id: string, patch: Partial<ModelConfig>) => void;
    47   deleteModel: (id: string) => void;
    48   generateImage: (params: GenerateImageParams) => Promise<GenerateImageResponse>;
    49   testModel: (model: ModelConfig) => Promise<boolean>;
    50   saving: boolean;
    51 }
    52 
    53 const ModelContext = createContext<ModelContextValue | null>(null);
    54 
    55 const STORAGE_KEY = 'ai_model_configs';
    56 
    57 function sanitizeModel(m: Partial<ModelConfig>): ModelConfig {
    58   return {
    59     id:         m.id         || uuidv4(),
    60     name:       m.name       || '未命名模型',
    61     modelName:  m.modelName  || '',
    62     baseUrl:    m.baseUrl    || '',
    63     apiKey:     m.apiKey     || '',
    64     enabled:    m.enabled    !== undefined ? m.enabled : false,
    65     type:       (['gpt-image','dalle','tongyi','custom','video'] as const).includes(m.type as never)
    66                   ? (m.type as ModelConfig['type'])
    67                   : 'custom',
    68     isDefault:  m.isDefault  || false,
    69   };
    70 }
    71 
    72 function loadLocalModels(): ModelConfig[] {
    73   try {
    74     const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    75     if (!raw) return DEFAULT_MODELS;
    76     const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
    77     if (!Array.isArray(parsed) || parsed.length === 0) return DEFAULT_MODELS;
    78     return parsed.map(sanitizeModel);
    79   } catch {
    80     return DEFAULT_MODELS;
    81   }
    82 }
    83 
    84 function saveLocalModels(models: ModelConfig[]) {
    85   try {
    86     localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(models));
    87   } catch {
    88     // 忽略存储错误
    89   }
    90 }
    91 
    92 export function ModelProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
    93   const { user, profile } = useAuth();
    94   const [models, setModels] = useState<ModelConfig[]>(loadLocalModels);
    95   const [activeModelId, setActiveModelIdState] = useState<string>(() => {
    96     return localStorage.getItem('ai_active_model') || 'gpt-image-2';
    97   });
    98   const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
    99 
   100   // 从 profile 同步远端配置（合并写法，避免多次 setModels 导致竞态）
   101   useEffect(() => {
   102     if (!profile) return;
   103     try {
   104       setModels((prev) => {
   105         let base = prev;
   106         // 用远端覆盖本地（若有效）
   107         if (profile.model_configs && Array.isArray(profile.model_configs) && profile.model_configs.length > 0) {
   108           base = (profile.model_configs as Partial<ModelConfig>[]).map(sanitizeModel);
   109           saveLocalModels(base);
   110         }
   111         // 同步 api_key 到 gpt-image-2
   112         if (profile.api_key) {
   113           return base.map((m) => m.id === 'gpt-image-2' ? { ...m, apiKey: profile.api_key! } : m);
   114         }
   115         return base;
   116       });
   117       if (profile.active_model_id) {
   118         setActiveModelIdState(profile.active_model_id);
   119       }
   120     } catch (e) {
   121       console.error('[ModelContext] 同步 profile 数据失败:', e);
   122     }
   123   }, [profile]);
   124 
   125   const persistToDb = useCallback(async (updated: ModelConfig[], newActiveId?: string) => {
   126     if (!user) return;
   127     setSaving(true);
   128     const { error } = await supabase
   129       .from('profiles')
   130       .update({
   131         model_configs: updated,
   132         ...(newActiveId ? { active_model_id: newActiveId } : {}),
   133       })
   134       .eq('id', user.id);
   135     setSaving(false);
   136     if (error) console.error('[ModelContext] 保存模型配置失败:', error.message);
   137   }, [user]);
   138 
   139   const setActiveModelId = useCallback((id: string) => {
   140     setActiveModelIdState(id);
   141     localStorage.setItem('ai_active_model', id);
   142     if (user) persistToDb(models, id);
   143   }, [user, models, persistToDb]);
   144 
   145   const addModel = useCallback((model: Omit<ModelConfig, 'id'>) => {
   146     const newModel: ModelConfig = { ...model, id: uuidv4() };
   147     const updated = [...models, newModel];
   148     setModels(updated);
   149     saveLocalModels(updated);
   150     persistToDb(updated);
   151   }, [models, persistToDb]);
   152 
   153   const updateModel = useCallback((id: string, patch: Partial<ModelConfig>) => {
   154     const updated = models.map((m) => m.id === id ? { ...m, ...patch } : m);
   155     setModels(updated);
   156     saveLocalModels(updated);
   157     persistToDb(updated);
   158     // 同步到 profile.api_key（仅 gpt-image-2 主模型）
   159     if (id === 'gpt-image-2' && patch.apiKey !== undefined && user) {
   160       supabase.from('profiles').update({ api_key: patch.apiKey }).eq('id', user.id).then(({ error }) => {
   161         if (error) console.error('[ModelContext] 同步 api_key 失败:', error.message);
   162       });
   163     }
   164   }, [models, persistToDb, user]);
   165 
   166   const deleteModel = useCallback((id: string) => {
   167     const updated = models.filter((m) => m.id !== id);
   168     setModels(updated);
   169     saveLocalModels(updated);
   170     persistToDb(updated);
   171     if (activeModelId === id) {
   172       const fallback = updated.find((m) => m.enabled)?.id || '';
   173       setActiveModelId(fallback);
   174     }
   175   }, [models, activeModelId, persistToDb, setActiveModelId]);
   176 
   177   const activeModel = models.find((m) => m.id === activeModelId) || models.find((m) => m.enabled) || null;
   178 
   179   // 单次模型调用
   180   async function callModel(model: ModelConfig, params: GenerateImageParams): Promise<GenerateImageResponse> {
   181     if (!model.apiKey) throw new Error(`模型 "${model.name}" 尚未配置 API Key`);
   182 
   183     const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('generate-image', {
   184       body: {
   185         prompt: params.prompt,
   186         // GrsAI gpt-image-2 使用比例格式的 size（如 '3:2'），参数名为 variants
   187         size: params.size || '1:1',
   188         variants: params.variants ?? 1,
   189       },
   190       headers: {
   191         'x-api-key': model.apiKey,
   192         'x-base-url': model.baseUrl,
   193         'x-model-name': model.modelName,
   194       },
   195     });
   196 
   197     if (error) {
   198       const raw = await error?.context?.text().catch(() => '');
   199       let msg = error.message;
   200       try { msg = (JSON.parse(raw ?? '')).error || msg; } catch { /* noop */ }
   201       console.error(`[ModelContext] ${model.name} 调用失败:`, msg);
   202       throw new Error(msg);
   203     }
   204 
   205     if (!data?.success) throw new Error(data?.error || '生成失败');
   206     return data as GenerateImageResponse;
   207   }
   208 
   209   // 带 fallback 的多模型调度
   210   const generateImage = useCallback(async (params: GenerateImageParams): Promise<GenerateImageResponse> => {
   211     const enabledModels = models.filter((m) => m.enabled && m.apiKey);
   212     if (enabledModels.length === 0) {
   213       return { success: false, error: '未找到可用模型，请先配置 API Key 并启用模型' };
   214     }
   215 
   216     // 主模型优先
   217     const primary = enabledModels.find((m) => m.id === activeModelId) || enabledModels[0];
   218     const fallbacks = enabledModels.filter((m) => m.id !== primary.id);
   219     const queue = [primary, ...fallbacks];
   220 
   221     let lastError = '';
   222     for (const model of queue) {
   223       try {
   224         console.log(`[ModelContext] 使用模型: ${model.name}`);
   225         const result = await callModel(model, params);
   226         if (result.success) {
   227           if (model.id !== primary.id) {
   228             toast.info(`主模型失败，已切换至 ${model.name}`);
   229           }
   230           return result;
   231         }
   232         lastError = result.error || '未知错误';
   233       } catch (err) {
   234         lastError = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   235         console.warn(`[ModelContext] ${model.name} 失败，尝试下一个模型: ${lastError}`);
   236       }
   237     }
   238     return { success: false, error: lastError || '所有模型均失败，请检查 API Key 和网络' };
   239   }, [models, activeModelId]);
   240 
   241   // 测试模型连接
   242   const testModel = useCallback(async (model: ModelConfig): Promise<boolean> => {
   243     try {
   244       const result = await callModel(model, {
   245         prompt: 'a simple test image, white background',
   246         size: '1:1',
   247         variants: 1,
   248       });
   249       return result.success;
   250     } catch {
   251       return false;
   252     }
   253   }, []);
   254 
   255   return (
   256     <ModelContext.Provider value={{
   257       models, activeModel, activeModelId, setActiveModelId,
   258       addModel, updateModel, deleteModel,
   259       generateImage, testModel, saving,
   260     }}>
   261       {children}
   262     </ModelContext.Provider>
   263   );
   264 }
   265 
   266 export function useModel() {
   267   const ctx = useContext(ModelContext);
   268   if (!ctx) throw new Error('useModel must be used within ModelProvider');
   269   return ctx;
   270 }

    13 function pixelSizeToRatio(size: string): string {
    14   const r: Record<string, string> = {
    15     '1792x1024': '3:2',
    16     '1024x768':  '4:3',
    17     '1024x1024': '1:1',
    18     '1024x1792': '2:3',
    19     '1792x768':  '3:2',
    20   };
    21   return r[size] || '3:2';
    22 }

    24 interface ImageItem {
    25   url?: string;
    26   uri?: string;
    27   b64_json?: string;

    50 // ─── 带超时的 fetch ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    51 async function fetchWithTimeout(
    52   url: string,
    53   options: RequestInit,
    54   timeoutMs: number,
    55 ): Promise<Response> {
    56   const controller = new AbortController();
    57   const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs);
    58   try {
    59     return await fetch(url, { ...options, signal: controller.signal });
    60   } finally {
    61     clearTimeout(timeoutId);
    62   }
    63 }
    64 
    65 // ─── 带重试（5xx 重试，4xx 不重试）────────────────────────────────────────────
    66 async function fetchWithRetry(
    67   url: string,
    68   options: RequestInit,
    69   maxRetries: number,
    70   timeoutMs: number,
    71 ): Promise<Response> {
    72   let lastError: Error = new Error('未知错误');
    73   for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++) {
    74     try {
    75       console.log(`[generate-image] 第 ${attempt}/${maxRetries} 次请求`);
    76       const response = await fetchWithTimeout(url, options, timeoutMs);
    77       if (response.ok || (response.status >= 400 && response.status < 500)) {
    78         return response;
    79       }
    80       lastError = new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
    81     } catch (err) {
    82       lastError = err instanceof Error ? err : new Error(String(err));
    83       if (lastError.name === 'AbortError') {
    84         lastError = new Error(`请求超时（${timeoutMs / 1000}秒），请检查网络或稍后重试`);
    85       }
    86       console.warn(`[generate-image] 第 ${attempt} 次异常: ${lastError.message}`);
    87     }
    88     if (attempt < maxRetries) {
    89       await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, attempt * 2000));
    90     }
    91   }
    92   throw lastError;
    93 }
    94 
    95 // ─── 核心：逐字符解析拼接的多 JSON 对象流 ────────────────────────────────────
    96 // grsai 响应格式: {"id":"..."}{"status":"running"}{"status":"succeeded","results":[...]}
    97 // 标准 JSON.parse 会在这种格式上失败，需要按花括号深度逐段切割
    98 function parseStreamingJson(raw: string): GrsaiChunk[] {
    99   const cleaned = raw.replace(/^\uFEFF/, '').trim();
   100   if (!cleaned) return [];
   101 
   102   // 检测 HTML 错误页（网关/CDN 返回）
   103   if (cleaned.startsWith('<!') || cleaned.toLowerCase().startsWith('<html')) {
   104     const title = cleaned.match(/<title[^>]*>(.*?)<\/title>/i)?.[1] || '';
   105     throw new Error(`服务返回 HTML 错误页${title ? `: ${title}` : ''}，请检查 API 地址`);
   106   }
   107 
   108   const chunks: GrsaiChunk[] = [];
   109   let depth = 0;
   110   let start = -1;
   111   let inString = false;
   112   let escape = false;
   113 
   114   for (let i = 0; i < cleaned.length; i++) {
   115     const ch = cleaned[i];
   116 
   117     // 字符串内转义处理
   118     if (escape) { escape = false; continue; }
   119     if (ch === '\\' && inString) { escape = true; continue; }
   120     if (ch === '"') { inString = !inString; continue; }
   121     if (inString) continue;
   122 
   123     if (ch === '{') {
   124       if (depth === 0) start = i;
   125       depth++;
   126     } else if (ch === '}') {
   127       depth--;
   128       if (depth === 0 && start !== -1) {
   129         const fragment = cleaned.slice(start, i + 1);
   130         try {
   131           chunks.push(JSON.parse(fragment) as GrsaiChunk);
   132         } catch {
   133           console.warn(`[generate-image] 跳过无效片段: ${fragment.slice(0, 80)}`);
   134         }
   135         start = -1;
   136       }
   137     }
   138   }
   139 
   140   return chunks;
   141 }
   142 
   143 // ─── 从最终 chunk 中判断是否成功并提取图片 URL ────────────────────────────────
   144 
   145 // 宽松的成功判断：兼容 grsai 所有可能的 status/code 字段
   146 function isSuccessChunk(chunk: GrsaiChunk): boolean {
   147   // status 字符串全覆盖
   148   const status = String(chunk.status ?? '').toLowerCase();
   149   if (['succeeded', 'success', 'done', 'complete', 'completed', 'finished', 'ok', '200'].includes(status)) return true;
   150 
   151   // 数字/字符串 code：0 或 200 视为成功
   152   const code = chunk.code;
   153   if (code === 0 || code === '0' || code === 200 || code === '200') return true;
   154 
   155   // progress >= 100
   156   if (typeof chunk.progress === 'number' && chunk.progress >= 100) return true;
   157 
   158   // 含图片数据的数组字段（只要非空就算成功）
   159   if (Array.isArray(chunk.results) && chunk.results.length > 0) return true;
   160   if (Array.isArray(chunk.data)    && chunk.data.length > 0)    return true;
   161   if (Array.isArray(chunk.images)  && chunk.images.length > 0)  return true;
   162   if (Array.isArray(chunk.output)  && chunk.output.length > 0)  return true;
   163 
   164   // 顶层直接有 URL
   165   if (typeof chunk.url === 'string' && chunk.url.startsWith('http')) return true;
   166 
   167   return false;
   168 }
   169 
   170 // 递归深度扫描：找到任意一个 http(s) URL 字符串
   171 function deepFindUrl(obj: unknown, depth = 0): string | undefined {
   172   if (depth > 6) return undefined;
   173   if (typeof obj === 'string') {
   174     return (obj.startsWith('http://') || obj.startsWith('https://')) ? obj : undefined;
   175   }
   176   if (Array.isArray(obj)) {
   177     for (const item of obj) {
   178       const found = deepFindUrl(item, depth + 1);
   179       if (found) return found;
   180     }
   181   }
   182   if (obj && typeof obj === 'object') {
   183     // 优先检查高概率字段
   184     const priorityKeys = ['url', 'uri', 'image_url', 'imageUrl', 'src', 'link'];
   185     const rec = obj as Record<string, unknown>;
   186     for (const k of priorityKeys) {
   187       const found = deepFindUrl(rec[k], depth + 1);
   188       if (found) return found;
   189     }
   190     // 再扫描其余字段
   191     for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(rec)) {
   192       if (priorityKeys.includes(k)) continue;
   193       const found = deepFindUrl(v, depth + 1);
   194       if (found) return found;
   195     }
   196   }
   197   return undefined;
   198 }
   199 
   200 function extractImageUrl(chunk: GrsaiChunk): string | undefined {
   201   // grsai 格式：results[0].url 或 results[0].uri
   202   if (Array.isArray(chunk.results) && chunk.results.length > 0) {
   203     return chunk.results[0].url || chunk.results[0].uri;
   204   }
   205   // OpenAI 标准：data[0].url
   206   if (Array.isArray(chunk.data) && chunk.data.length > 0) {
   207     return (chunk.data as ImageItem[])[0]?.url;
   208   }
   209   // 其他兼容格式
   210   if (Array.isArray(chunk.images) && chunk.images.length > 0) return chunk.images[0].url;
   211   if (Array.isArray(chunk.output) && chunk.output.length > 0) return (chunk.output[0] as ImageItem).url;
   212   if (typeof chunk.url === 'string' && chunk.url.startsWith('http')) return chunk.url;
   213   return undefined;
   214 }
   215 
   216 function extractB64(chunk: GrsaiChunk): string | undefined {
   217   if (Array.isArray(chunk.results) && chunk.results.length > 0) return chunk.results[0].b64_json;
   218   if (Array.isArray(chunk.data) && chunk.data.length > 0) return (chunk.data as ImageItem[])[0]?.b64_json;
   219   if (typeof chunk.b64_json === 'string' && chunk.b64_json) return chunk.b64_json;
   220   return undefined;
   221 }
   222 
   223 // ─── 将英文 API 错误翻译为用户友好的中文提示 ──────────────────────────────────
   224 function friendlyErrorMessage(raw: string): string {
   225   const s = raw.toLowerCase();
   226   if (s.includes('insufficient credits') || s.includes('insufficient balance') ||
   227       s.includes('quota exceeded') || s.includes('rate limit') ||
   228       s.includes('billing') || s.includes('credit')) {
   229     return `API 余额不足，请前往 grsai 平台为账户充值后重试（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   230   }
   231   if (s.includes('invalid api key') || s.includes('unauthorized') ||
   232       s.includes('authentication') || s.includes('api key')) {
   233     return `API Key 无效或已过期，请在设置页面重新配置（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   234   }
   235   if (s.includes('content policy') || s.includes('safety') ||
   236       s.includes('violated') || s.includes('blocked')) {
   237     return `提示词触发内容安全限制，请修改描述后重试（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   238   }
   239   if (s.includes('timeout') || s.includes('timed out')) {
   240     return `请求超时，请稍后重试（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   241   }
   242   return raw;
   243 }
   244 
   245 // ─── 从错误 chunk 中提取可读信息 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   246 function extractErrorMessage(chunk: GrsaiChunk, httpStatus: number): string {
   247   let raw = '';
   248   if (chunk.error) {
   249     if (typeof chunk.error === 'object') {
   250       raw = chunk.error.message || chunk.error.msg || JSON.stringify(chunk.error);
   251     } else if (typeof chunk.error === 'string') {
   252       raw = chunk.error;
   253     }
   254   }
   255   if (!raw && typeof chunk.message === 'string') raw = chunk.message;
   256   if (!raw && typeof chunk.msg    === 'string') raw = chunk.msg;
   257   if (!raw && typeof chunk.detail === 'string') raw = chunk.detail;
   258   if (!raw) return `API 请求失败 (HTTP ${httpStatus})`;
   259   return friendlyErrorMessage(raw);
   260 }

   262 // ─── Edge Function 入口 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   263 serve(async (req: Request) => {
   264   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
   265     return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });
   266   }
   267 
   268   const jsonResp = (body: unknown, status = 200) =>
   269     new Response(JSON.stringify(body), {
   270       status,
   271       headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   272     });
   273 
   274   try {
   275     const apiKey = req.headers.get('x-api-key');
   276     if (!apiKey) {
   277       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '未提供 API Key，请在设置页面配置' }, 401);
   278     }
   279 
   280     const baseUrl = req.headers.get('x-base-url') || DEFAULT_ENDPOINT;
   281     const modelName = req.headers.get('x-model-name') || 'gpt-image-2';
   282 
   283     let body: Record<string, unknown>;
   284     try {
   285       body = await req.json();
   286     } catch {
   287       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请求体 JSON 格式错误' }, 400);
   288     }
   289 
   290     const {
   291       prompt,
   292       size = '1:1',
   293       n = 1,
   294       variants = 1,
   295       response_format = 'url',
   296     } = body as {
   297       prompt?: string;
   298       size?: string;
   299       n?: number;
   300       variants?: number;
   301       response_format?: string;
   302     };
   303 
   304     if (!prompt?.trim()) {
   305       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请输入图片描述' }, 400);
   306     }
   307 
   308     // GrsAI gpt-image-2：size 使用比例格式，参数名为 variants，移除 style 等不支持字段
   309     const requestPayload = {
   310       model: modelName,
   311       prompt: prompt.trim(),
   312       variants: Number(variants) || Number(n) || 1,
   313       size: pixelSizeToRatio(String(size)),
   314       response_format: String(response_format),
   315     };
   316 
   317     console.log(`[generate-image] endpoint=${baseUrl} model=${modelName} size=${size}`);
   318     console.log(`[generate-image] prompt=${String(prompt).slice(0, 80)}`);
   319 
   320     // ── 发起请求 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   321     let response: Response;
   322     try {
   323       response = await fetchWithRetry(
   324         baseUrl,
   325         {
   326           method: 'POST',
   327           headers: {
   328             'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   329             'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   330           },
   331           body: JSON.stringify(requestPayload),
   332         },
   333         MAX_RETRIES,
   334         REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS,
   335       );
   336     } catch (err) {
   337       const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   338       console.error(`[generate-image] 所有重试失败: ${msg}`);
   339       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: msg }, 503);
   340     }

   343     console.log(`[generate-image] HTTP ${response.status}，响应前600字: ${rawText.slice(0, 600)}`);
   344 
   345     // ── 解析流式 JSON 响应 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   346     let chunks: GrsaiChunk[];
   347     try {
   348       chunks = parseStreamingJson(rawText);
   349     } catch (parseErr) {
   350       const msg = parseErr instanceof Error ? parseErr.message : String(parseErr);
   351       console.error(`[generate-image] 响应解析失败: ${msg}`);
   352       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: msg }, 502);
   353     }
   354 
   355     console.log(`[generate-image] 解析得到 ${chunks.length} 个 JSON 片段`);
   356 
   357     if (chunks.length === 0) {
   358       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '服务返回空响应，请稍后重试' }, 502);
   359     }
   360 
   361     // ── HTTP 4xx/5xx 错误：从第一个 chunk 提取错误信息 ───────────────────────
   362     if (!response.ok) {
   363       const errMsg = extractErrorMessage(chunks[0], response.status);
   364       console.error(`[generate-image] API 错误(${response.status}): ${errMsg}`);
   365       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: errMsg }, response.status);
   366     }
   367

   376 
   377     if (successChunk) {
   378       const imageUrl = extractImageUrl(successChunk);

   383       }
   384     }
   385

   387     for (const chunk of [...chunks].reverse()) {
   388       const url = deepFindUrl(chunk);

```
  const handleSaveProfile = async (values: ProfileValues) => {
    if (!profile) return;
    setProfileSaving(true);
    const { error } = await supabase.from('profiles').update({ api_key: values.apiKey }).eq('id', profile.id);
    setProfileSaving(false);
    if (error) { toast.error(`保存失败：${error.message}`); return; }
```

```
    profileForm.reset({ apiKey: values.apiKey });
```

问题：用户保存 API Key 后跳转到编辑器页，"生成图片"按钮仍处于禁用状态（`hasApiKey` 为 false）。

原因是 `const hasApiKey = !!(activeModel?.apiKey || profile?.api_key);` 这一行只在 render 时计算，当用户从设置页跳转过来时，`activeModel` 的 `apiKey` 还没同步。

修复：在 AIGenerator 组件中添加一个 useEffect，当 `profile.api_key` 变化时，将 API Key 同步到 localStorage 中（因为 ModelContext 的 `useEffect` 从 localStorage 读取 models）。在 return 之前、生成按钮上方添加此 useEffect。

请在 `const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);` 之后（第97行附近）插入以下代码：

```
  // 同步 profile 中的 api_key 到 localStorage 兜底
  useEffect(() => {
    if (profile?.api_key) {
      try {
        const stored = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ai_model_configs) || []);
        const updated = stored.map((m: any) =>
          m.id === gpt-image-2 ? { ...m, apiKey: profile.api_key } : m
        );
        localStorage.setItem(ai_model_configs, JSON.stringify(updated));
      } catch { /* noop */ }
    }
  }, [profile?.api_key]);
```

```
  useEffect(() => {
    if (profile?.api_key) {
      try {
        const stored = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ai_model_configs') || '[]');
        const updated = stored.map((m: { id: string; apiKey?: string }) =>
          m.id === 'gpt-image-2' ? { ...m, apiKey: profile.api_key } : m
        );
        localStorage.setItem('ai_model_configs', JSON.stringify(updated));
      } catch { /* noop */ }
    }
  }, [profile?.api_key]);
```

AgentThinkAction(thought='I notice something important in SettingsPage.tsx: the `useEffect` on line 168-171 references `profileForm`, but `profileForm` is declared on line 173 - AFTER the useEffect. This is a bug - `profileForm` is used before it\'s declared. In JavaScript/React, this would cause a "Cannot access \'profileForm\' before initialization" error at runtime because `useForm` returns a new object each render, and hooks must be called in the same order.\n\nActually wait - in React hooks, the order matters and all hooks are called on every render. `useState` and `useForm` (which uses useState internally) are called before `useEffect` runs. So the declarations are evaluated in order: `useState` for profileSaving, then `useEffect` is registered (not executed yet), then `useForm` runs. When the component renders, all hooks run in order, and the effect only runs AFTER the render. So `profileForm` will be defined by the time the effect runs.\n\nBUT - there\'s still an issue: JavaScript uses temporal dead zones for `const`. The `useEffect` callback captures `profileForm` via closure. Since `profileForm` is declared with `const` after `useEffect`, this is actually a temporal dead zone issue. The closure captures `profileForm` which at the time the `useEffect` is registered is... wait.\n\nActually, React hooks work differently. The `useEffect` callback is a closure. The `profileForm` variable in the closure refers to the binding in the outer function scope. When `useEffect(() => { profileForm.reset... }, [profile?.api_key])` is called, the `profileForm` variable exists because by that point in the execution, `useEffect` is just registering the callback, not executing it. The callback will execute asynchronously after render, at which point `profileForm` will be in scope and initialized.\n\nActually, in JavaScript with `const`, variables are in the temporal dead zone until the line where they\'re declared is reached during execution. But `useEffect` just registers a callback - it doesn\'t execute it. The callback itself is a closure over the entire function scope. When the callback eventually runs (after the component renders), all the `const` declarations in the function body have already been executed, so `profileForm` will be defined.\n\nBut the linter would normally flag this as "react-hooks/exhaustive-deps" or similar. Looking at the code, the `eslint-disable-line` comment already handles that.\n\nActually, thinking about it more carefully - in JavaScript closures over `const` in function bodies, the closure captures the variable binding, not the value. All `const` declarations in a function are hoisted to the top of their scope (but in TDZ until initialized). When the `useEffect` callback runs, it will access `profileForm` from the same scope. Since by the time `useEffect`\'s callback runs (after render), `profileForm` will have been initialized, this should work fine.\n\nBut wait - there could be an issue with `useForm` returning a stable reference. `profileForm` is declared with `const profileForm = useForm(...)` - `useForm` from react-hook-form returns a stable object reference across renders. So the closure will always have access to the same form instance.\n\nActually, I\'m overthinking this. The real concern is: does this code work? Let me check if linting passes - it does. So there\'s no issue there.\n\nThe main thing the user wants is for the CDN to update. The best I can do is make a real code change (even minor) to ensure the build produces new file hashes, then publish.\n\nLet me make a small but real improvement: move the `useEffect` to be after `profileForm` declaration, which is actually more correct code ordering (even though it works either way). This will definitely change the file content and produce a new bundle hash.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

CONTENT: 请修复 src/components/PPTEditor.tsx 中的 addNewSlide 函数闪退问题。

根因：点击"新增"按钮触发状态更新后，React 重渲染时 Radix UI 的 Popover/Select 组件发生 Portal removeChild 时序错误，ErrorBoundary 虽然自动恢复了，但状态更新丢失，幻灯片没有实际加上。

修复方法：将 addNewSlide 中的状态更新用 setTimeout(0) 包裹，避免与当前渲染周期的 Portal 卸载冲突。

当前代码（约第430行）：
```
  const addNewSlide = () => {
    const newSlide: Slide = { id: uuidv4(), background: #0F111A, elements: [], order: data.slides.length };
    onChange({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
    setActiveSlideIndex(data.slides.length);
    setSelectedElement(null);
  };
```

改为：
```
  const addNewSlide = () => {
    const newSlide: Slide = { id: uuidv4(), background: #0F111A, elements: [], order: data.slides.length };
    setTimeout(() => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
      setActiveSlideIndex(data.slides.length);
      setSelectedElement(null);
    }, 0);
  };
```

完成后直接发布到生产环境（先确保代码正确提交，再发布）。告诉我新版本号。

<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.USER)
CONTENT: 修复 src/components/PPTEditor.tsx 中点击"新增"闪退问题。

根因已确认：页面的"背景"按钮使用 Radix Popover 组件，它创建 Portal DOM 节点。当新增幻灯片触发重渲染时，Portal 的 DOM 卸载时机与 React 提交阶段冲突导致 removeChild 错误。

修复方法：在 addNewSlide 中用 requestAnimationFrame 代替 setTimeout(0)，让浏览器先完成当前帧的 Portal 清理，再触发状态更新。

当前代码（addNewSlide 函数）：
```
  const addNewSlide = () => {
    const newSlide: Slide = { id: uuidv4(), background: #0F111A, elements: [], order: data.slides.length };
    setTimeout(() => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
      setActiveSlideIndex(data.slides.length);
      setSelectedElement(null);
    }, 0);
  };
```

改为：
```
  const addNewSlide = () => {
    const newSlide: Slide = { id: uuidv4(), background: #0F111A, elements: [], order: data.slides.length };
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
      setActiveSlideIndex(data.slides.length);
      setSelectedElement(null);
    });
  };
```

另外，同样检查 deleteSlide、duplicateSlide 函数是否也有类似问题，如有也加上 requestAnimationFrame。

修改完成后直接发布到生产环境。告诉我新版本号和 CDN bundle 文件名（index-*.js）。
</action>

```
    });
  };

  const deleteSlide = (index: number) => {
    if (data.slides.length <= 1) return;
    const newSlides = data.slides.filter((_, i) => i !== index);
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: newSlides.map((s, i) => ({ ...s, order: i })) });
      setActiveSlideIndex(Math.min(index, newSlides.length - 1));
      setSelectedElement(null);
    });
  };

  // 第2项：复制幻灯片
  const duplicateSlide = (index: number) => {
    const sorted = [...data.slides].sort((a, b) => a.order - b.order);
    const src = sorted[index];
    if (!src) return;
    const copy: Slide = {
      ...src,
      id: uuidv4(),
      elements: src.elements.map((el) => ({ ...el, id: uuidv4() })),
      order: index + 1,
    };
    const newSlides = [
      ...sorted.slice(0, index + 1),
      copy,
      ...sorted.slice(index + 1),
    ].map((s, i) => ({ ...s, order: i }));
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: newSlides });
      setActiveSlideIndex(index + 1);
      setSelectedElement(null);
    });
  };
```

</action>

<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.USER)
CONTENT: 修复 src/components/PPTEditor.tsx 中点击"新增幻灯片"按钮闪退问题。

根因：页面工具栏中的"背景"按钮使用 Radix Popover 组件（创建 Portal DOM 节点）。当新增幻灯片触发 React 重渲染时，Portal 的 DOM 卸载与 React 提交阶段冲突，抛出 removeChild 错误。ErrorBoundary 虽然恢复了，但导致整个页面组件重新挂载，状态丢失，幻灯片加不上。

修复方案：给 addNewSlide 和 deleteSlide 函数加 try-catch，如果捕获到 removeChild 错误，延迟 200ms 后重试操作。ErrorBoundary 的 auto-recovery 会在 100ms 内完成，200ms 后重试时组件已恢复。

当前 addNewSlide（约第430行）：
```
  const addNewSlide = () => {
    const newSlide: Slide = { id: uuidv4(), background: #0F111A, elements: [], order: data.slides.length };
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
      setActiveSlideIndex(data.slides.length);
      setSelectedElement(null);
    });
  };
```

改为：
```
  const addNewSlide = () => {
    const newSlide: Slide = { id: uuidv4(), background: #0F111A, elements: [], order: data.slides.length };
    try {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
    } catch (e) {
      if ((e as Error)?.message?.includes(removeChild)) {
        // Portal removeChild 冲突，等 ErrorBoundary 恢复后重试
        setTimeout(() => {
          setPptDataRef.current?.({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
        }, 200);
      } else throw e;
    }
    setActiveSlideIndex(data.slides.length);
    setSelectedElement(null);
  };
```

另外 deleteSlide 也要同样处理。

请直接在当前文件上修改，修改完成后发布到生产环境。

发布后告诉我新版本号。
</action>

```
  const addNewSlide = () => {
    const newSlide: Slide = { id: uuidv4(), background: '#0F111A', elements: [], order: data.slides.length };
    const applyAdd = () => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: [...data.slides, newSlide] });
      setActiveSlideIndex(data.slides.length);
      setSelectedElement(null);
    };
    try {
      applyAdd();
    } catch (e) {
      if ((e as Error)?.message?.includes('removeChild')) {
        // Portal removeChild 冲突，等 ErrorBoundary 恢复后重试（100ms 内完成）
        setTimeout(applyAdd, 200);
      } else {
        throw e;
      }
    }
  };

  const deleteSlide = (index: number) => {
    if (data.slides.length <= 1) return;
    const newSlides = data.slides.filter((_, i) => i !== index);
    const applyDelete = () => {
      onChange({ ...data, slides: newSlides.map((s, i) => ({ ...s, order: i })) });
      setActiveSlideIndex(Math.min(index, newSlides.length - 1));
      setSelectedElement(null);
    };
    try {
      applyDelete();
    } catch (e) {
      if ((e as Error)?.message?.includes('removeChild')) {
        setTimeout(applyDelete, 200);
      } else {
        throw e;
      }
    }
  };
```

**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.USER)
CONTENT: 请在项目中创建一个新的 Supabase Edge Function：parse-docx。功能：用户上传 .docx 文件，解析内容后调用 DeepSeek API 生成结构化 JSON 用于 PPT 生成。

创建 supabase/functions/parse-docx/index.ts，功能如下：

1. 接受 multipart/form-data 上传的 .docx 文件
2. 使用 Deno 内置库解析 Word 文档（用 mammoth npm 包提取文本）
3. 将提取的文本片段发送给 DeepSeek API（用户配置的 DeepSeek API Key）
4. DeepSeek 的 prompt 要求输出结构化 JSON：
{
  "slides": [
    {
      "type": "cover" | "section" | "content" | "ending",
      "title": "幻灯片标题",
      "subtitle": "副标题（可选）",
      "image_prompt": "英文生图提示词，用于后续 AI 配图",
      "bullets": ["要点1", "要点2", "要点3"]
    }
  ]
}
- 每页 3~5 个要点
- image_prompt 自动根据页面内容生成英文描述

5. 实现 CORS 支持
6. 返回 JSON：{ success: true, slides: [...] } 或 { success: false, error: '...' }

技术要点：
- 使用 Deno 兼容的方式解析 Word（使用 mammoth 的 ESM 版本）
- DeepSeek API 端点：https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions
- 模型：deepseek-chat
- API Key 从请求体中读取（类似 generate-image 的方式）
- 超时 120 秒
- 支持从请求 Authorization header 或 body.apiKey 读取 API Key
- 请求前先验证 API Key 是否存在
- 响应支持中文字段

注意：新建的 parse-docx 文件夹放在 supabase/functions/ 下。请新建文件不要修改已有文件。

const DEFAULT_ENDPOINT = 'https://grsai.dakka.com.cn/v1/draw/completions';
const REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 90000;
const MAX_RETRIES = 2;

function pixelSizeToRatio(size: string): string {
  const r: Record<string, string> = {
    '1792x1024': '3:2',
    '1024x768':  '4:3',
    '1024x1024': '1:1',
    '1024x1792': '2:3',
    '1792x768':  '3:2',
  };
  return r[size] || '3:2';
}

```
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.168.0/http/server.ts";
// @deno-types="npm:@types/mammoth"
import mammoth from "npm:mammoth";

const corsHeaders = {
  'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type, x-api-key',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
};

const DEEPSEEK_ENDPOINT = 'https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions';
const DEEPSEEK_MODEL = 'deepseek-chat';
const REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 120000;

// ─── 带超时的 fetch ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function fetchWithTimeout(
  url: string,
  options: RequestInit,
  timeoutMs: number,
): Promise<Response> {
  const controller = new AbortController();
  const id = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs);
  try {
    return await fetch(url, { ...options, signal: controller.signal });
  } finally {
    clearTimeout(id);
  }
}

// ─── 从 Word 文件 Buffer 提取纯文本 ──────────────────────────────────────────
async function extractTextFromDocx(buffer: ArrayBuffer): Promise<string> {
  const result = await mammoth.extractRawText({ arrayBuffer: buffer });
  return result.value.trim();
}

// ─── 调用 DeepSeek 生成结构化幻灯片 JSON ─────────────────────────────────────
async function generateSlidesFromText(text: string, apiKey: string): Promise<unknown> {
  const systemPrompt = `你是一位专业的 PPT 内容设计师，擅长将文档内容转化为结构清晰、逻辑连贯的演示文稿。`;

  const userPrompt = `请将以下文档内容转化为 PPT 幻灯片结构，严格按照 JSON 格式输出，不要输出任何其他内容。

要求：
1. 根据内容合理划分幻灯片，通常 8~15 页
2. 第一页为封面（type: "cover"），最后一页为结束页（type: "ending"）
3. 章节分隔页使用 type: "section"，正文内容页使用 type: "content"
4. 每页 bullets 3~5 个要点，简洁有力
5. image_prompt 用英文描述该页适合配的图片风格，便于 AI 生图
6. 所有文字字段（title/subtitle/bullets）使用中文

输出格式（只输出 JSON，不要 markdown 代码块）：
{
  "slides": [
    {
      "type": "cover",
      "title": "幻灯片主标题",
      "subtitle": "副标题或日期（可选）",
      "image_prompt": "English prompt for AI image generation",
      "bullets": []
    },
    {
      "type": "content",
      "title": "章节标题",
      "subtitle": "",
      "image_prompt": "English prompt for AI image generation",
      "bullets": ["要点1", "要点2", "要点3"]
    }
  ]
}

文档内容：
${text.slice(0, 12000)}`;

  const resp = await fetchWithTimeout(
    DEEPSEEK_ENDPOINT,
    {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: DEEPSEEK_MODEL,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
          { role: 'user', content: userPrompt },
        ],
        temperature: 0.7,
        max_tokens: 4096,
      }),
    },
    REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS,
  );

  if (!resp.ok) {
    const errText = await resp.text();
    throw new Error(`DeepSeek API 错误 ${resp.status}: ${errText}`);
  }

  const json = await resp.json();
  const content: string = json?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content ?? '';
  if (!content) throw new Error('DeepSeek 返回内容为空');

  // 清理可能包含的 markdown 代码块标记
  const cleaned = content.replace(/^```(?:json)?\s*/i, '').replace(/\s*```$/i, '').trim();

  try {
    return JSON.parse(cleaned);
  } catch {
    throw new Error(`DeepSeek 返回格式无法解析：${cleaned.slice(0, 200)}`);
  }
}

// ─── 主处理逻辑 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
serve(async (req: Request) => {
  // CORS 预检
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  if (req.method !== 'POST') {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '仅支持 POST 请求' }),
      { status: 405, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
    );
  }

  try {
    // 读取 multipart/form-data
    const contentType = req.headers.get('content-type') ?? '';
    if (!contentType.includes('multipart/form-data')) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '请使用 multipart/form-data 上传文件' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    const formData = await req.formData();
    const file = formData.get('file') as File | null;
    const apiKeyFromBody = formData.get('apiKey') as string | null;

    // 从 Authorization header 读取（Bearer token 格式）或 body 中读取
    const authHeader = req.headers.get('authorization') ?? '';
    const apiKeyFromHeader = authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')
      ? authHeader.slice(7).trim()
      : (req.headers.get('x-api-key') ?? '');

    const apiKey = (apiKeyFromBody || apiKeyFromHeader || '').trim();

    // 验证 API Key
    if (!apiKey) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '未提供 DeepSeek API Key，请在设置中配置' }),
        { status: 401, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    // 验证文件
    if (!file) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '未找到上传的文件，请上传 .docx 文件' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    const fileName = file.name?.toLowerCase() ?? '';
    if (!fileName.endsWith('.docx')) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '仅支持 .docx 格式的 Word 文档' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    // 解析 Word 文档
    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
    const text = await extractTextFromDocx(arrayBuffer);

    if (!text || text.length < 10) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '文档内容为空或无法提取文本，请检查文件' }),
        { status: 422, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    // 调用 DeepSeek 生成结构化 JSON
    const parsed = await generateSlidesFromText(text, apiKey) as { slides?: unknown[] };
    const slides = parsed?.slides;

    if (!Array.isArray(slides) || slides.length === 0) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: 'AI 未能生成有效的幻灯片内容，请重试' }),
        { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ success: true, slides }),
      { status: 200, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
    );

  } catch (err: unknown) {
    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
    console.error('[parse-docx] 错误：', message);
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: message }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
    );
  }
});

```

<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.USER)
CONTENT: 请在项目中创建新的组件文件 src/components/DocGenerator.tsx，功能是让用户上传 Word 文档，调用 parse-docx Edge Function 解析，然后一键生成 PPT 幻灯片。

这个组件放在 AI 面板里作为新的 Tab。完整代码：

```tsx
import { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { useModel } from '@/contexts/ModelContext';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';
import type { Slide, SlideElement } from '@/types/types';

interface DocGeneratorProps {
  onSlidesGenerated: (slides: Slide[], title: string) => void;
}

interface ParsedSlide {
  type: string;
  title: string;
  subtitle?: string;
  image_prompt?: string;
  bullets?: string[];
}

export default function DocGenerator({ onSlidesGenerated }: DocGeneratorProps) {
  const { profile } = useAuth();
  const { models } = useModel();
  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  const [file, setFile] = useState<File | null>(null);
  const [parsing, setParsing] = useState(false);
  const [parseProgress, setParseProgress] = useState(0);
  const [parsedSlides, setParsedSlides] = useState<ParsedSlide[] | null>(null);
  const [pptTitle, setPptTitle] = useState('');
  const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false);
  const deepseekKey = profile?.api_key || '';
  const hasKey = !!deepseekKey;

  const handleFileSelect = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const f = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!f) return;
    if (!f.name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.docx')) {
      toast.error('仅支持 .docx 格式的 Word 文档');
      return;
    }
    setFile(f);
    setPptTitle(f.name.replace(/\.docx$/i, ''));
    setParsedSlides(null);
  };

  const handleParse = async () => {
    if (!file) { toast.error('请先选择 Word 文档'); return; }
    if (!hasKey) { toast.error('请先在设置页面配置 DeepSeek API Key'); return; }
    setParsing(true);
    setParseProgress(10);
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      setParseProgress((p) => (p < 85 ? p + Math.random() * 8 : p));
    }, 400);
    try {
      setParseProgress(50);
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('file', file);
      formData.append('apiKey', deepseekKey);
      const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('parse-docx', { body: formData });
      if (error) {
        const errText = await error?.context?.text?.()?.catch(() => '');
        throw new Error(errText || error.message || '解析失败');
      }
      if (!data?.success) throw new Error(data?.error || '解析失败');
      setParseProgress(100);
      const slides = data.slides as ParsedSlide[];
      setParsedSlides(slides);
      toast.success('解析成功！共 ' + slides.length + ' 页幻灯片');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error('解析失败：' + (err instanceof Error ? err.message : '未知错误'));
    } finally {
      clearInterval(timer);
      setParsing(false);
      setTimeout(() => setParseProgress(0), 600);
    }
  };

  const handleGeneratePPT = () => {
    if (!parsedSlides || parsedSlides.length === 0) return;
    setGenerating(true);
    try {
      const bgColor = '#0F111A';
      const textColor = '#e5e5e5';
      const subtitleColor = '#6b7280';
      const accentColor = '#6366f1';
      const slides: Slide[] = parsedSlides.map((ps, idx) => {
        const elements: SlideElement[] = [];
        let yOffset = 8;
        if (ps.type === 'cover' && idx === 0) {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 25, width: 90, height: 18, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title, fontSize: 42, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'center' });
          if (ps.subtitle) elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 10, y: 48, width: 80, height: 10, zIndex: 2, text: ps.subtitle, fontSize: 20, fontColor: subtitleColor, fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'center' });
        } else if (ps.type === 'section') {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 30, width: 90, height: 15, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title, fontSize: 36, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'center' });
          if (ps.subtitle) elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 10, y: 50, width: 80, height: 8, zIndex: 2, text: ps.subtitle, fontSize: 16, fontColor: subtitleColor, fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'center' });
        } else {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 5, width: 90, height: 10, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title, fontSize: 28, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'left' });
          yOffset = 17;
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'shape', x: 5, y: yOffset, width: 30, height: 0.3, zIndex: 1, shapeType: 'rect', fillColor: accentColor });
          yOffset += 5;
          (ps.bullets || []).forEach((bullet, bi) => {
            elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 8, y: yOffset, width: 84, height: 6, zIndex: 2, text: (bi + 1) + '. ' + bullet, fontSize: 16, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'left' });
            yOffset += 8;
          });
        }
        if (ps.type === 'ending') {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 35, width: 90, height: 15, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title || '感谢聆听', fontSize: 40, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'center' });
        }
        if (idx > 0) {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 85, y: 92, width: 12, height: 5, zIndex: 1, text: '' + (idx + 1), fontSize: 10, fontColor: '#4b5563', fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'right' });
        }
        return { id: uuidv4(), background: ps.type === 'cover' ? 'linear-gradient(135deg, #0F111A 0%, #1a1a3e 100%)' : bgColor, elements, order: idx };
      });
      onSlidesGenerated(slides, pptTitle || 'Word 导入文稿');
      toast.success('PPT 已生成！');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error('生成失败：' + (err instanceof Error ? err.message : '未知错误'));
    } finally { setGenerating(false); }
  };

  const slideTypes: Record<string, string> = {
    cover: '封面', section: '章节页', content: '内容页', ending: '结束页',
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full text-foreground">
      <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-border">
        <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">Word 文稿导入</h2>
        <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">上传 Word 文档，自动生成 PPT</p>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4 space-y-4">
        {!hasKey && (
          <div className="p-3 rounded-lg border border-border bg-accent text-xs text-accent-foreground">
            请前往 <a href="/settings" className="underline font-medium">设置</a> 配置 DeepSeek API Key
          </div>
        )}
        <div>
          <button type="button" onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()} className="w-full border border-dashed border-border hover:border-muted-foreground rounded-lg p-6 text-center transition-colors cursor-pointer">
            {file ? (
              <div className="space-y-1"><p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">{file.name}</p><p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">{(file.size / 1024).toFixed(0)} KB</p></div>
            ) : (
              <div className="space-y-1"><p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">点击上传 Word 文档</p><p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground/50">支持 .docx 格式</p></div>
            )}
          </button>
          <input ref={fileInputRef} type="file" accept=".docx,application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document" className="hidden" onChange={handleFileSelect} />
        </div>
        {file && (
          <div>
            <label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1.5 block">PPT 标题</label>
            <input type="text" value={pptTitle} onChange={(e) => setPptTitle(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-8 px-2.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-secondary border border-border text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground/60 focus:border-ring focus:outline-none" placeholder="输入 PPT 标题..." />
          </div>
        )}
        {file && !parsedSlides && (
          <button type="button" onClick={handleParse} disabled={parsing || !hasKey} className="w-full py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-semibold transition-all duration-150 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed btn-accent">
            {parsing ? (
              <span className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2"><span className="w-3.5 h-3.5 border-2 border-current/30 border-t-current rounded-full animate-spin" />AI 解析中...</span>
            ) : 'AI 解析文档'}
          </button>
        )}
        {parseProgress > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-1"><Progress value={parseProgress} className="h-1 bg-secondary" /><p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground text-right">{Math.round(parseProgress)}%</p></div>
        )}
        {parsedSlides && parsedSlides.length > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-3 slide-up">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between"><label className="text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">解析结果：共 {parsedSlides.length} 页</label></div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5 max-h-52 overflow-y-auto pr-1">
              {parsedSlides.map((s, i) => (
                <div key={i} className="p-2.5 rounded-lg bg-secondary/60 border border-border text-xs space-y-0.5">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5"><span>{slideTypes[s.type] || '页面'}</span><span className="text-muted-foreground">.</span><span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate flex-1">{s.title}</span></div>
                  {s.bullets && s.bullets.length > 0 && <p className="text-muted-foreground text-[10px] line-clamp-1">{s.bullets.slice(0, 2).join(' . ')}{s.bullets.length > 2 && '...'}</p>}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            <button type="button" onClick={handleGeneratePPT} disabled={generating} className="w-full py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-semibold transition-all duration-150 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed ai-breathing">
              {generating ? <span className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2"><span className="w-3.5 h-3.5 border-2 border-current/30 border-t-current rounded-full animate-spin" />生成 PPT 中...</span> : '一键生成 PPT'}
            </button>
            <button type="button" onClick={() => { setFile(null); setParsedSlides(null); setPptTitle(''); }} className="w-full py-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors">重新选择文件</button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

创建文件路径：src/components/DocGenerator.tsx（新文件，不要修改已有文件）。

然后修改 src/pages/CreatePage.tsx：
1. 添加 import: import DocGenerator from '@/components/DocGenerator';
2. 在 AITab 类型中添加 'doc': type AITab = 'image' | 'video' | 'doc';
3. 在 handleImageGenerated 后面添加 handleSlidesGenerated 回调
4. 在 Tab 按钮中把 ['image', 'video'] 改为 ['image', 'video', 'doc']
5. 在 AI 面板内容区添加 doc Tab 分支

注意：只添加，不删除已有代码。不要修改 image/video 相关代码逻辑。

   249                       <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" d="m2.25 15.75 5.159-5.159a2.25 2.25 0 0 1 3.182 0l5.159 5.159m-1.5-1.5 1.409-1.409a2.25 2.25 0 0 1 3.182 0l2.909 2.909m-18 3.75h16.5a1.5 1.5 0 0 0 1.5-1.5V6a1.5 1.5 0 0 0-1.5-1.5H3.75A1.5 1.5 0 0 0 2.25 6v12a1.5 1.5 0 0 0 1.5 1.5Zm10.5-11.25h.008v.008h-.008V8.25Zm.375 0a.375.375 0 1 1-.75 0 .375.375 0 0 1 .75 0Z" />
   250                     </svg>
   251                     图片生成
   252                   </>
   253                 ) : (
   254                   <>
   255                     <svg className="w-3.5 h-3.5" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth={1.5}>

   257                     </svg>
   258                     视频生成
   259                   </>
   260                 )}
   261               </button>
   262             ))}
   263           </div>
   264           {/* 内容区 */}

   268             ) : (

   270             )}

   273

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-b7xiaa8vv30h/src/components/DocGenerator.tsx]
Thought: 现在掌握了全貌，开始创建组件并修改 CreatePage：
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
import { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { useModel } from '@/contexts/ModelContext';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';
import type { Slide, SlideElement } from '@/types/types';

interface DocGeneratorProps {
  onSlidesGenerated: (slides: Slide[], title: string) => void;
}

interface ParsedSlide {
  type: string;
  title: string;
  subtitle?: string;
  image_prompt?: string;
  bullets?: string[];
}

export default function DocGenerator({ onSlidesGenerated }: DocGeneratorProps) {
  const { profile } = useAuth();
  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars
  const { models } = useModel();
  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  const [file, setFile] = useState<File | null>(null);
  const [parsing, setParsing] = useState(false);
  const [parseProgress, setParseProgress] = useState(0);
  const [parsedSlides, setParsedSlides] = useState<ParsedSlide[] | null>(null);
  const [pptTitle, setPptTitle] = useState('');
  const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false);
  const deepseekKey = profile?.api_key || '';
  const hasKey = !!deepseekKey;

  const handleFileSelect = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const f = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!f) return;
    if (!f.name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.docx')) {
      toast.error('仅支持 .docx 格式的 Word 文档');
      return;
    }
    setFile(f);
    setPptTitle(f.name.replace(/\.docx$/i, ''));
    setParsedSlides(null);
  };

  const handleParse = async () => {
    if (!file) { toast.error('请先选择 Word 文档'); return; }
    if (!hasKey) { toast.error('请先在设置页面配置 DeepSeek API Key'); return; }
    setParsing(true);
    setParseProgress(10);
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      setParseProgress((p) => (p < 85 ? p + Math.random() * 8 : p));
    }, 400);
    try {
      setParseProgress(50);
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('file', file);
      formData.append('apiKey', deepseekKey);
      const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('parse-docx', { body: formData });
      if (error) {
        const errText = await error?.context?.text?.()?.catch(() => '');
        throw new Error(errText || error.message || '解析失败');
      }
      if (!data?.success) throw new Error(data?.error || '解析失败');
      setParseProgress(100);
      const slides = data.slides as ParsedSlide[];
      setParsedSlides(slides);
      toast.success('解析成功！共 ' + slides.length + ' 页幻灯片');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error('解析失败：' + (err instanceof Error ? err.message : '未知错误'));
    } finally {
      clearInterval(timer);
      setParsing(false);
      setTimeout(() => setParseProgress(0), 600);
    }
  };

  const handleGeneratePPT = () => {
    if (!parsedSlides || parsedSlides.length === 0) return;
    setGenerating(true);
    try {
      const bgColor = '#0F111A';
      const textColor = '#e5e5e5';
      const subtitleColor = '#6b7280';
      const accentColor = '#6366f1';
      const slides: Slide[] = parsedSlides.map((ps, idx) => {
        const elements: SlideElement[] = [];
        let yOffset = 8;
        if (ps.type === 'cover' && idx === 0) {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 25, width: 90, height: 18, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title, fontSize: 42, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'center' });
          if (ps.subtitle) elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 10, y: 48, width: 80, height: 10, zIndex: 2, text: ps.subtitle, fontSize: 20, fontColor: subtitleColor, fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'center' });
        } else if (ps.type === 'section') {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 30, width: 90, height: 15, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title, fontSize: 36, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'center' });
          if (ps.subtitle) elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 10, y: 50, width: 80, height: 8, zIndex: 2, text: ps.subtitle, fontSize: 16, fontColor: subtitleColor, fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'center' });
        } else if (ps.type === 'ending') {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 35, width: 90, height: 15, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title || '感谢聆听', fontSize: 40, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'center' });
        } else {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 5, y: 5, width: 90, height: 10, zIndex: 2, text: ps.title, fontSize: 28, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'bold', fontAlign: 'left' });
          yOffset = 17;
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'shape', x: 5, y: yOffset, width: 30, height: 0.3, zIndex: 1, shapeType: 'rect', fillColor: accentColor });
          yOffset += 5;
          (ps.bullets || []).forEach((bullet, bi) => {
            elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 8, y: yOffset, width: 84, height: 6, zIndex: 2, text: (bi + 1) + '. ' + bullet, fontSize: 16, fontColor: textColor, fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'left' });
            yOffset += 8;
          });
        }
        if (idx > 0) {
          elements.push({ id: uuidv4(), type: 'text', x: 85, y: 92, width: 12, height: 5, zIndex: 1, text: '' + (idx + 1), fontSize: 10, fontColor: '#4b5563', fontWeight: 'normal', fontAlign: 'right' });
        }
        return {
          id: uuidv4(),
          background: ps.type === 'cover' ? 'linear-gradient(135deg, #0F111A 0%, #1a1a3e 100%)' : bgColor,
          elements,
          order: idx,
        };
      });
      onSlidesGenerated(slides, pptTitle || 'Word 导入文稿');
      toast.success('PPT 已生成！');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error('生成失败：' + (err instanceof Error ? err.message : '未知错误'));
    } finally {
      setGenerating(false);
    }
  };

  const slideTypeLabels: Record<string, string> = {
    cover: '封面',
    section: '章节页',
    content: '内容页',
    ending: '结束页',
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full text-foreground">
      {/* 头部 */}
      <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-border shrink-0">
        <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">Word 文稿导入</h2>
        <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">上传 Word 文档，自动生成 PPT</p>
      </div>

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4 space-y-4">
        {/* 未配置 Key 提示 */}
        {!hasKey && (
          <div className="p-3 rounded-lg border border-border bg-accent text-xs text-accent-foreground">
            请前往 <a href="/settings" className="underline font-medium">设置</a> 配置 DeepSeek API Key
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 文件上传区 */}
        <div>
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}
            className="w-full border border-dashed border-border hover:border-muted-foreground rounded-lg p-6 text-center transition-colors cursor-pointer"
          >
            {file ? (
              <div className="space-y-1">
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">{file.name}</p>
                <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">{(file.size / 1024).toFixed(0)} KB</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="space-y-1">
                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">点击上传 Word 文档</p>
                <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground/50">支持 .docx 格式</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </button>
          <input
            ref={fileInputRef}
            type="file"
            accept=".docx,application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document"
            className="hidden"
            onChange={handleFileSelect}
          />
        </div>

        {/* PPT 标题输入 */}
        {file && (
          <div>
            <label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1.5 block">PPT 标题</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={pptTitle}
              onChange={(e) => setPptTitle(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full h-8 px-2.5 text-xs rounded-md bg-secondary border border-border text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground/60 focus:border-ring focus:outline-none"
              placeholder="输入 PPT 标题..."
            />
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 解析按钮 */}
        {file && !parsedSlides && (
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={handleParse}
            disabled={parsing || !hasKey}
            className="w-full py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-semibold transition-all duration-150 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed btn-accent"
          >
            {parsing ? (
              <span className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
                <span className="w-3.5 h-3.5 border-2 border-current/30 border-t-current rounded-full animate-spin" />
                AI 解析中...
              </span>
            ) : 'AI 解析文档'}
          </button>
        )}

        {/* 解析进度条 */}
        {parseProgress > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <Progress value={parseProgress} className="h-1 bg-secondary" />
            <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground text-right">{Math.round(parseProgress)}%</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 解析结果预览 + 生成按钮 */}
        {parsedSlides && parsedSlides.length > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <label className="text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">
                解析结果：共 {parsedSlides.length} 页
              </label>
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5 max-h-52 overflow-y-auto pr-1">
              {parsedSlides.map((s, i) => (
                <div key={i} className="p-2.5 rounded-lg bg-secondary/60 border border-border text-xs space-y-0.5">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                    <span className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0">{slideTypeLabels[s.type] || '页面'}</span>
                    <span className="text-muted-foreground">·</span>
                    <span className="font-medium text-foreground truncate flex-1">{s.title}</span>
                  </div>
                  {s.bullets && s.bullets.length > 0 && (
                    <p className="text-muted-foreground text-[10px] line-clamp-1">
                      {s.bullets.slice(0, 2).join(' · ')}{s.bullets.length > 2 && '...'}
                    </p>
                  )}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={handleGeneratePPT}
              disabled={generating}
              className="w-full py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-semibold transition-all duration-150 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed ai-breathing"
            >
              {generating ? (
                <span className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
                  <span className="w-3.5 h-3.5 border-2 border-current/30 border-t-current rounded-full animate-spin" />
                  生成 PPT 中...
                </span>
              ) : '一键生成 PPT'}
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => { setFile(null); setParsedSlides(null); setPptTitle(''); }}
              className="w-full py-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors"
            >
              重新选择文件
            </button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.USER)
CONTENT: 请在 supabase/functions/ 目录下创建一个新的 Edge Function，命名为 parse-docx，用于解析 Word (.docx) 文件并调用 DeepSeek API 结构化输出。

请创建文件 supabase/functions/parse-docx/index.ts，内容如下（注意：这是一个完整的文件，请完全替换为新文件）：

```typescript
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.168.0/http/server.ts";
import JSZip from "https://deno.land/x/jszip@0.11.0/mod.ts";

const corsHeaders = {
  'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
};

const DEEPSEEK_API = 'https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions';
const REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 120000;

const EXTRACT_PROMPT = `你是一个PPT内容结构化专家。从以下Word文稿文本中提取发布会PPT的内容结构，输出严格JSON格式：

{
  "slides": [
    {
      "type": "类型",
      "title": "页面标题",
      "subtitle": "副标题文字（可选）",
      "image_prompt": "英文图片描述，用于AI生图",
      "bullets": ["要点1", "要点2", "要点3"]
    }
  ]
}

规则：
1. 第一页type="cover"作为封面，包含标题、副标题
2. 正文页type="content"，每页3~5个要点
3. 最后一页type="ending"作为结束页
4. image_prompt用英文描述适合该页的背景/配图
5. 只输出JSON，不要任何解释文字`;

interface SlideJson {
  type: string;
  title: string;
  subtitle?: string;
  image_prompt: string;
  bullets: string[];
}

interface ParseResult {
  success: boolean;
  data?: { slides: SlideJson[] };
  error?: string;
  rawText?: string;
}

/** 从 docx ZIP 中提取纯文本 */
async function extractTextFromDocx(buffer: Uint8Array): Promise<string> {
  const zip = await JSZip.loadAsync(buffer);
  const docFile = zip.file('word/document.xml');
  if (!docFile) throw new Error('无法找到 word/document.xml，文件可能不是有效的 .docx');

  const xmlText = await docFile.async('string');
  // 使用 DOMParser 解析 XML
  const parser = new DOMParser();
  const doc = parser.parseFromString(xmlText, 'text/xml');

  // 提取所有 <w:t> 标签内的文本
  const textElements = doc.getElementsByTagNameNS('*', 't');
  const paragraphs: string[] = [];
  let currentPara = '';

  for (const el of textElements) {
    const text = el.textContent || '';
    currentPara += text;
    // 检查是否到达段落末尾（下一个兄弟元素判断）
    const parent = el.parentNode;
    if (parent) {
      const nextSibling = el.nextSibling;
      if (!nextSibling || (nextSibling.nodeType === 3 && (nextSibling.textContent || '').trim() === '')) {
        // Check if this is the last <w:t> in this paragraph
        const nextT = parent.querySelector(':scope > w\\:r + w\\:r w\\:t, :scope > r + r t');
        if (!nextT) {
          if (currentPara.trim()) paragraphs.push(currentPara.trim());
          currentPara = '';
        }
      }
    }
  }

  if (currentPara.trim()) paragraphs.push(currentPara.trim());

  // Fallback: also try getting all <w:p> elements and concatenating their <w:t> children
  if (paragraphs.length === 0) {
    const pElements = doc.getElementsByTagNameNS('*', 'p');
    for (const p of pElements) {
      const tElements = p.getElementsByTagNameNS('*', 't');
      let paraText = '';
      for (const t of tElements) {
        paraText += t.textContent || '';
      }
      if (paraText.trim()) paragraphs.push(paraText.trim());
    }
  }

  return paragraphs.join('\n');
}

/** 调用 DeepSeek API 结构化文本 */
async function callDeepSeek(text: string, apiKey: string): Promise<SlideJson[]> {
  const response = await fetch(DEEPSEEK_API, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: 'deepseek-chat',
      messages: [
        { role: 'system', content: EXTRACT_PROMPT },
        { role: 'user', content: text },
      ],
      temperature: 0.1,
      max_tokens: 4096,
    }),
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const errText = await response.text();
    throw new Error(`DeepSeek API 错误 (${response.status}): ${errText.slice(0, 200)}`);
  }

  const result = await response.json();
  const content = result.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || '';

  // 提取 JSON（可能被 ```json ... ``` 包裹）
  const jsonMatch = content.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/) || content.match(/{[\s\S]*}/);
  const jsonStr = jsonMatch ? jsonMatch[1] || jsonMatch[0] : content;

  const parsed = JSON.parse(jsonStr);
  if (parsed.slides && Array.isArray(parsed.slides)) {
    return parsed.slides as SlideJson[];
  }
  throw new Error('DeepSeek 返回格式不符合预期：缺少 slides 数组');
}

serve(async (req: Request) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  const jsonResp = (body: unknown, status = 200) =>
    new Response(JSON.stringify(body), {
      status,
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });

  try {
    // Parse body - supports JSON or formData
    let body: Record<string, unknown>;
    let fileBuffer: Uint8Array | null = null;
    let deepseekApiKey = '';
    let textContent = '';

    const contentType = req.headers.get('content-type') || '';

    if (contentType.includes('multipart/form-data')) {
      // FormData upload
      const formData = await req.formData();
      const file = formData.get('file') as File | null;
      deepseekApiKey = (formData.get('apiKey') as string) || '';

      if (!file) {
        return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请上传 .docx 文件' }, 400);
      }

      const arrayBuf = await file.arrayBuffer();
      fileBuffer = new Uint8Array(arrayBuf);
    } else {
      // JSON body
      try {
        body = await req.json();
      } catch {
        const text = await req.text();
        body = JSON.parse(text);
      }

      deepseekApiKey = (body.apiKey as string) || '';

      // Accept base64 file content
      if (body.fileBase64) {
        const b64 = body.fileBase64 as string;
        const binaryStr = atob(b64);
        fileBuffer = new Uint8Array(binaryStr.length);
        for (let i = 0; i < binaryStr.length; i++) {
          fileBuffer[i] = binaryStr.charCodeAt(i);
        }
      }

      // Accept direct text content
      if (body.text) {
        textContent = body.text as string;
      }
    }

    if (!fileBuffer && !textContent) {
      return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请提供 .docx 文件或文本内容' }, 400);
    }

    // Extract text from docx or use provided text
    const rawText = fileBuffer ? await extractTextFromDocx(fileBuffer) : textContent;

    if (!rawText.trim()) {
      return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '未能从文档中提取到文本内容' }, 400);
    }

    console.log(`[parse-docx] 提取到 ${rawText.length} 字符文本`);

    // If no API key provided, return the raw text for frontend preview
    if (!deepseekApiKey) {
      return jsonResp({
        success: true,
        info: '未提供 DeepSeek API Key，仅返回提取的文本',
        rawText: rawText.slice(0, 2000),
        slides: null,
      });
    }

    // Call DeepSeek to structure the content
    const slides = await callDeepSeek(rawText, deepseekApiKey);

    console.log(`[parse-docx] DeepSeek 返回 ${slides.length} 页幻灯片`);

    return jsonResp({
      success: true,
      slides,
      rawText: rawText.slice(0, 500),
    });

  } catch (error: unknown) {
    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : '未知错误';
    console.error('[parse-docx] 错误:', errorMessage);
    return jsonResp({ success: false, error: errorMessage }, 500);
  }
});
```

    15 async function fetchWithTimeout(
    16   url: string,
    17   options: RequestInit,
    18   timeoutMs: number,
    19 ): Promise<Response> {
    20   const controller = new AbortController();
    21   const id = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs);
    22   try {
    23     return await fetch(url, { ...options, signal: controller.signal });
    24   } finally {
    25     clearTimeout(id);
    26   }
    27 }
