```
// ─── 带超时的 fetch ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function fetchWithTimeout(
  url: string,
  options: RequestInit,
  timeoutMs: number,
): Promise<Response> {
  const controller = new AbortController();
  const id = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs);
  try {
    return await fetch(url, { ...options, signal: controller.signal });
  } finally {
    clearTimeout(id);
  }
}

// ─── 从 Word 文件 Buffer 提取纯文本 ──────────────────────────────────────────
async function extractTextFromDocx(buffer: ArrayBuffer): Promise<string> {
  const result = await mammoth.extractRawText({ arrayBuffer: buffer });
  return result.value.trim();
}

// ─── 调用 DeepSeek 生成结构化幻灯片 JSON ─────────────────────────────────────
async function generateSlidesFromText(text: string, apiKey: string): Promise<unknown> {
  const systemPrompt = `你是一位专业的 PPT 内容设计师，擅长将文档内容转化为结构清晰、逻辑连贯的演示文稿。`;

  const userPrompt = `请将以下文档内容转化为 PPT 幻灯片结构，严格按照 JSON 格式输出，不要输出任何其他内容。

要求：
1. 根据内容合理划分幻灯片，通常 8~15 页
2. 第一页为封面（type: "cover"），最后一页为结束页（type: "ending"）
3. 章节分隔页使用 type: "section"，正文内容页使用 type: "content"
4. 每页 bullets 3~5 个要点，简洁有力
5. image_prompt 用英文描述该页适合配的图片风格，便于 AI 生图
6. 所有文字字段（title/subtitle/bullets）使用中文

输出格式（只输出 JSON，不要 markdown 代码块）：
{
  "slides": [
    {
      "type": "cover",
      "title": "幻灯片主标题",
      "subtitle": "副标题或日期（可选）",
      "image_prompt": "English prompt for AI image generation",
      "bullets": []
    },
    {
      "type": "content",
      "title": "章节标题",
      "subtitle": "",
      "image_prompt": "English prompt for AI image generation",
      "bullets": ["要点1", "要点2", "要点3"]
    }
  ]
}

文档内容：
${text.slice(0, 12000)}`;

  const resp = await fetchWithTimeout(
    DEEPSEEK_ENDPOINT,
    {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: DEEPSEEK_MODEL,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
          { role: 'user', content: userPrompt },
        ],
        temperature: 0.7,
        max_tokens: 4096,
      }),
    },
    REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS,
  );

  if (!resp.ok) {
    const errText = await resp.text();
    throw new Error(`DeepSeek API 错误 ${resp.status}: ${errText}`);
  }

  const json = await resp.json();
  const content: string = json?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content ?? '';
  if (!content) throw new Error('DeepSeek 返回内容为空');

  // 清理可能包含的 markdown 代码块标记
  const cleaned = content.replace(/^```(?:json)?\s*/i, '').replace(/\s*```$/i, '').trim();

  try {
    return JSON.parse(cleaned);
  } catch {
    throw new Error(`DeepSeek 返回格式无法解析：${cleaned.slice(0, 200)}`);
  }
}

// ─── 主处理逻辑 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
serve(async (req: Request) => {
  // CORS 预检
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  if (req.method !== 'POST') {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '仅支持 POST 请求' }),
      { status: 405, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
    );
  }

  try {
    // 读取 multipart/form-data
    const contentType = req.headers.get('content-type') ?? '';
    if (!contentType.includes('multipart/form-data')) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '请使用 multipart/form-data 上传文件' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    const formData = await req.formData();
    const file = formData.get('file') as File | null;
    const apiKeyFromBody = formData.get('apiKey') as string | null;

    // 从 Authorization header 读取（Bearer token 格式）或 body 中读取
    const authHeader = req.headers.get('authorization') ?? '';
    const apiKeyFromHeader = authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')
      ? authHeader.slice(7).trim()
      : (req.headers.get('x-api-key') ?? '');

    const apiKey = (apiKeyFromBody || apiKeyFromHeader || '').trim();

    // 验证 API Key
    if (!apiKey) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '未提供 DeepSeek API Key，请在设置中配置' }),
        { status: 401, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    // 验证文件
    if (!file) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '未找到上传的文件，请上传 .docx 文件' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    const fileName = file.name?.toLowerCase() ?? '';
    if (!fileName.endsWith('.docx')) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '仅支持 .docx 格式的 Word 文档' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    // 解析 Word 文档
    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
    const text = await extractTextFromDocx(arrayBuffer);

    if (!text || text.length < 10) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: '文档内容为空或无法提取文本，请检查文件' }),
        { status: 422, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    // 调用 DeepSeek 生成结构化 JSON
    const parsed = await generateSlidesFromText(text, apiKey) as { slides?: unknown[] };
    const slides = parsed?.slides;

    if (!Array.isArray(slides) || slides.length === 0) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: 'AI 未能生成有效的幻灯片内容，请重试' }),
        { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
      );
    }

    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ success: true, slides }),
      { status: 200, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
    );

  } catch (err: unknown) {
    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
    console.error('[parse-docx] 错误：', message);
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: message }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } },
    );
  }
});
```

New String: ```
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.168.0/http/server.ts";
import JSZip from "https://deno.land/x/jszip@0.11.0/mod.ts";

const corsHeaders = {
  'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
};

const DEEPSEEK_API = 'https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions';
const REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 120000;

const EXTRACT_PROMPT = `你是一个PPT内容结构化专家。从以下Word文稿文本中提取发布会PPT的内容结构，输出严格JSON格式：

{
  "slides": [
    {
      "type": "类型",
      "title": "页面标题",
      "subtitle": "副标题文字（可选）",
      "image_prompt": "英文图片描述，用于AI生图",
      "bullets": ["要点1", "要点2", "要点3"]
    }
  ]
}

规则：
1. 第一页type="cover"作为封面，包含标题、副标题
2. 正文页type="content"，每页3~5个要点
3. 最后一页type="ending"作为结束页
4. image_prompt用英文描述适合该页的背景/配图
5. 只输出JSON，不要任何解释文字`;

interface SlideJson {
  type: string;
  title: string;
  subtitle?: string;
  image_prompt: string;
  bullets: string[];
}

/** 从 docx ZIP 中提取纯文本 */
async function extractTextFromDocx(buffer: Uint8Array): Promise<string> {
  const zip = await JSZip.loadAsync(buffer);
  const docFile = zip.file('word/document.xml');
  if (!docFile) throw new Error('无法找到 word/document.xml，文件可能不是有效的 .docx');

  const xmlText = await docFile.async('string');

  // 使用正则提取 <w:t> 标签内文本，按段落（<w:p>）组织
  const paragraphs: string[] = [];
  const paraRegex = /<w:p[ >][\s\S]*?<\/w:p>/g;
  const textRegex = /<w:t(?:\s[^>]*)?>([^<]*)<\/w:t>/g;

  let paraMatch: RegExpExecArray | null;
  while ((paraMatch = paraRegex.exec(xmlText)) !== null) {
    const paraXml = paraMatch[0];
    let paraText = '';
    let tMatch: RegExpExecArray | null;
    while ((tMatch = textRegex.exec(paraXml)) !== null) {
      paraText += tMatch[1];
    }
    textRegex.lastIndex = 0;
    if (paraText.trim()) paragraphs.push(paraText.trim());
  }

  return paragraphs.join('\n');
}

/** 调用 DeepSeek API 结构化文本 */
async function callDeepSeek(text: string, apiKey: string): Promise<SlideJson[]> {
  const controller = new AbortController();
  const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS);

  let response: Response;
  try {
    response = await fetch(DEEPSEEK_API, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: 'deepseek-chat',
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: EXTRACT_PROMPT },
          { role: 'user', content: text.slice(0, 12000) },
        ],
        temperature: 0.1,
        max_tokens: 4096,
      }),
      signal: controller.signal,
    });
  } finally {
    clearTimeout(timeoutId);
  }

  if (!response.ok) {
    const errText = await response.text();
    throw new Error(`DeepSeek API 错误 (${response.status}): ${errText.slice(0, 200)}`);
  }

  const result = await response.json();
  const content: string = result.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || '';
  if (!content) throw new Error('DeepSeek 返回内容为空');

  // 提取 JSON（兼容 ```json ... ``` 包裹）
  const jsonMatch = content.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/) || content.match(/(\{[\s\S]*\})/);
  const jsonStr = jsonMatch ? (jsonMatch[1] || jsonMatch[0]).trim() : content.trim();

  const parsed = JSON.parse(jsonStr);
  if (parsed.slides && Array.isArray(parsed.slides)) {
    return parsed.slides as SlideJson[];
  }
  throw new Error('DeepSeek 返回格式不符合预期：缺少 slides 数组');
}

// ─── 主处理逻辑 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
serve(async (req: Request) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  const jsonResp = (body: unknown, status = 200) =>
    new Response(JSON.stringify(body), {
      status,
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });

  try {
    let fileBuffer: Uint8Array | null = null;
    let deepseekApiKey = '';
    let textContent = '';

    const contentType = req.headers.get('content-type') || '';

    if (contentType.includes('multipart/form-data')) {
      // FormData 上传
      const formData = await req.formData();
      const file = formData.get('file') as File | null;
      deepseekApiKey = (formData.get('apiKey') as string) || '';

      if (!file) {
        return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请上传 .docx 文件' }, 400);
      }
      const arrayBuf = await file.arrayBuffer();
      fileBuffer = new Uint8Array(arrayBuf);
    } else {
      // JSON body
      let body: Record<string, unknown> = {};
      try {
        body = await req.json();
      } catch {
        const raw = await req.text();
        body = JSON.parse(raw);
      }

      deepseekApiKey = (body.apiKey as string) || '';

      // 支持 base64 文件内容
      if (body.fileBase64) {
        const b64 = body.fileBase64 as string;
        const binaryStr = atob(b64);
        fileBuffer = new Uint8Array(binaryStr.length);
        for (let i = 0; i < binaryStr.length; i++) {
          fileBuffer[i] = binaryStr.charCodeAt(i);
        }
      }

      // 支持直接传入文本
      if (body.text) {
        textContent = body.text as string;
      }
    }

    if (!fileBuffer && !textContent) {
      return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请提供 .docx 文件或文本内容' }, 400);
    }

    // 提取文本
    const rawText = fileBuffer ? await extractTextFromDocx(fileBuffer) : textContent;

    if (!rawText.trim()) {
      return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '未能从文档中提取到文本内容' }, 400);
    }

    console.log(`[parse-docx] 提取到 ${rawText.length} 字符文本`);

    // 未提供 API Key 时仅返回提取的文本
    if (!deepseekApiKey) {
      return jsonResp({
        success: true,
        info: '未提供 DeepSeek API Key，仅返回提取的文本',
        rawText: rawText.slice(0, 2000),
        slides: null,
      });
    }

    // 调用 DeepSeek 结构化
    const slides = await callDeepSeek(rawText, deepseekApiKey);
    console.log(`[parse-docx] DeepSeek 返回 ${slides.length} 页幻灯片`);

    return jsonResp({
      success: true,
      slides,
      rawText: rawText.slice(0, 500),
    });

  } catch (error: unknown) {
    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : '未知错误';
    console.error('[parse-docx] 错误:', errorMessage);
    return jsonResp({ success: false, error: errorMessage }, 500);
  }
});
```

    28 const MAX_FILE_SIZE = 1024 * 1024;
    29 
    30 async function compressImage(file: File, maxSize = MAX_FILE_SIZE): Promise<File> {
    31   return new Promise((resolve) => {
    32     const reader = new FileReader();
    33     reader.onload = (e) => {
    34       const img = new Image();
    35       img.onload = () => {
    36         let quality = 0.8;
    37         const maxDim = 1080;
    38         const scale = Math.min(1, maxDim / Math.max(img.width, img.height));
    39         const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    40         canvas.width = Math.round(img.width * scale);
    41         canvas.height = Math.round(img.height * scale);
    42         const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    43         if (!ctx) { resolve(file); return; }
    44         ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    45         const tryCompress = () => {
    46           canvas.toBlob((blob) => {
    47             if (!blob) { resolve(file); return; }
    48             if (blob.size <= maxSize || quality <= 0.1) {
    49               resolve(new File([blob], file.name.replace(/\.[^.]+$/, '.webp'), { type: 'image/webp' }));
    50             } else {
    51               quality -= 0.1;
    52               tryCompress();
    53             }
    54           }, 'image/webp', quality);
    55         };
    56         tryCompress();
    57       };
    58       img.src = e.target?.result as string;
    59     };
    60     reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    61   });
    62 }
    63 
    64 function SliderRow({ label, value, onChange, min = 0, max = 100 }: {
    65   label: string; value: number; onChange: (v: number) => void; min?: number; max?: number;
    66 }) {
    67   return (
    68     <div className="space-y-1.5">
    69       <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
    70         <Label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{label}</Label>
    71         <span className="text-xs tabular-nums text-muted-foreground w-6 text-right">{value}</span>
    72       </div>
    73       <Slider value={[value]} onValueChange={([v]) => onChange(v)} min={min} max={max} step={1} className="w-full" />
    74     </div>
    75   );
    76 }

    78 export default function AIGenerator({ onImageGenerated }: AIGeneratorProps) {
    79   const { profile } = useAuth();
    80   const { models, activeModel, activeModelId, setActiveModelId, generateImage } = useModel();
    81   const enabledModels = models.filter((m) => m.enabled);
    82 
    83   const [prompt, setPrompt] = useState('');
    84   const [negativePrompt, setNegativePrompt] = useState('');
    85   const [showAdvanced, setShowAdvanced] = useState(false);
    86   const [selectedSize, setSelectedSize] = useState<SizePreset>(SIZE_PRESETS[0]);
    87   const [customW, setCustomW] = useState('1024');
    88   const [customH, setCustomH] = useState('1024');
    89 
    90   const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false);
    91   const [genProgress, setGenProgress] = useState(0);
    92   const [generatedImages, setGeneratedImages] = useState<string[]>([]);
    93 
    94   const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);
    95   const [uploadProgress, setUploadProgress] = useState(0);
    96   const [uploadedFiles, setUploadedFiles] = useState<Array<{ name: string; url: string }>>([]);
    97   const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
    98 
    99   // 当 profile.api_key 变化时，同步到 localStorage 中的模型配置兜底
   100   // 确保从设置页跳转回来后 ModelContext 能立即读取到最新 apiKey
   101   useEffect(() => {
   102     if (profile?.api_key) {
   103       try {
   104         const stored = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ai_model_configs') || '[]');
   105         const updated = stored.map((m: { id: string; apiKey?: string }) =>
   106           m.id === 'gpt-image-2' ? { ...m, apiKey: profile.api_key } : m
   107         );
   108         localStorage.setItem('ai_model_configs', JSON.stringify(updated));
   109       } catch { /* noop */ }
   110     }
   111   }, [profile?.api_key]);
   112 
   113   const hasApiKey = !!(activeModel?.apiKey || profile?.api_key);
   114 
   115   const handleGenerate = async () => {
   116     if (!prompt.trim()) { toast.error('请输入图片描述'); return; }
   117     if (!hasApiKey) { toast.error('请先在设置页面为当前模型配置 API Key'); return; }
   118 
   119     setGenerating(true);
   120     setGenProgress(5);
   121     // 模拟生成进度（0→90%，完成后跳到100%）
   122     const timer = setInterval(() => {
   123       setGenProgress((p) => (p < 88 ? p + Math.random() * 8 : p));
   124     }, 400);
   125     try {
   126       // 直接使用 apiSize（像素格式），Edge Function 的 pixelSizeToRatio 会自动转换为比例格式
   127       const size = selectedSize.apiSize;
   128       const result = await generateImage({
   129         prompt: prompt.trim(),
   130         size,
   131         ...(negativePrompt.trim() ? { negativePrompt: negativePrompt.trim() } : {}),
   132       });
   133 
   134       if (!result.success) throw new Error(result.error || '生成失败');
   135 
   136       const urls: string[] = [];
   137       if (result.url) urls.push(result.url);
   138       if (result.images?.length) {
   139         result.images.forEach((img) => {
   140           const u = img.url || (img.b64_json ? `data:image/png;base64,${img.b64_json}` : '');
   141           if (u && !urls.includes(u)) urls.push(u);
   142         });
   143       }
   144       if (!urls.length) throw new Error('未获取到图片链接');
   145 
   146       setGeneratedImages(urls);
   147       setGenProgress(100);
   148       toast.success('图片生成成功');
   149     } catch (err) {
   150       toast.error(`生成失败：${err instanceof Error ? err.message : '未知错误'}`);
   151     } finally {
   152       clearInterval(timer);
   153       setGenerating(false);
   154       setTimeout(() => setGenProgress(0), 600);
   155     }
   156   };
   157 
   158   const handleFileUpload = async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
   159     const files = Array.from(e.target.files || []);
   160     if (!files.length) return;
   161     for (const file of files) {
   162       const allowed = ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/webp', 'application/pdf'];
   163       if (!allowed.includes(file.type)) {
   164         toast.error(`不支持的文件格式：${file.name}`);
   165         continue;
   166       }
   167       setUploading(true);
   168       setUploadProgress(20);
   169       try {
   170         let uploadFile = file;
   171         let compressed = false;
   172         if (file.type !== 'application/pdf' && file.size > MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
   173           uploadFile = await compressImage(file);
   174           compressed = true;
   175           toast.info(`已自动压缩至 ${(uploadFile.size / 1024).toFixed(0)} KB`);
   176         }
   177         setUploadProgress(60);
   178         const safeFilename = `${profile?.id}/${Date.now()}-${file.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]/g, '_')}`;
   179         const { data: uploadData, error } = await supabase.storage.from('uploads').upload(safeFilename, uploadFile, {
   180           contentType: uploadFile.type,
   181           upsert: false,
   182         });
   183         if (error) throw error;
   184         setUploadProgress(90);
   185         const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage.from('uploads').getPublicUrl(uploadData.path);
   186         setUploadedFiles((prev) => [...prev, { name: file.name, url: urlData.publicUrl }]);
   187         setUploadProgress(100);
   188         toast.success(`${compressed ? '(已压缩) ' : ''}上传成功：${file.name}`);
   189       } catch (err) {
   190         toast.error(`上传失败：${err instanceof Error ? err.message : '未知错误'}`);
   191       } finally {
   192         setUploading(false);
   193         setUploadProgress(0);
   194       }
   195     }
   196     e.target.value = '';
   197   };
   198 
   199   return (
   200     <div className="flex flex-col h-full text-foreground">
   201       {/* 标题 */}
   202       <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-border">
   203         <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold">AI 图片生成</h2>
   204         <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">输入描述，一键生成发布会配图</p>
   205       </div>
   206 
   207       <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4 space-y-4">
   208         {/* API Key 提示 */}
   209         {!hasApiKey && (
   210           <div className="p-3 rounded-lg border border-border bg-accent text-xs text-accent-foreground">
   211             请前往 <a href="/settings" className="underline font-medium">设置</a> 为模型配置 API Key
   212           </div>
   213         )}
   214 
   215         {/* 模型选择 */}

    50 // ─── 带超时的 fetch ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    51 async function fetchWithTimeout(
    52   url: string,
    53   options: RequestInit,
    54   timeoutMs: number,
    55 ): Promise<Response> {
    56   const controller = new AbortController();
    57   const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs);
    58   try {
    59     return await fetch(url, { ...options, signal: controller.signal });
    60   } finally {
    61     clearTimeout(timeoutId);
    62   }
    63 }
    64 
    65 // ─── 带重试（5xx 重试，4xx 不重试）────────────────────────────────────────────
    66 async function fetchWithRetry(
    67   url: string,
    68   options: RequestInit,
    69   maxRetries: number,
    70   timeoutMs: number,
    71 ): Promise<Response> {
    72   let lastError: Error = new Error('未知错误');
    73   for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++) {
    74     try {
    75       console.log(`[generate-image] 第 ${attempt}/${maxRetries} 次请求`);
    76       const response = await fetchWithTimeout(url, options, timeoutMs);
    77       if (response.ok || (response.status >= 400 && response.status < 500)) {
    78         return response;
    79       }
    80       lastError = new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
    81     } catch (err) {
    82       lastError = err instanceof Error ? err : new Error(String(err));
    83       if (lastError.name === 'AbortError') {
    84         lastError = new Error(`请求超时（${timeoutMs / 1000}秒），请检查网络或稍后重试`);
    85       }
    86       console.warn(`[generate-image] 第 ${attempt} 次异常: ${lastError.message}`);
    87     }
    88     if (attempt < maxRetries) {
    89       await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, attempt * 2000));
    90     }
    91   }
    92   throw lastError;
    93 }
    94 
    95 // ─── 核心：逐字符解析拼接的多 JSON 对象流 ────────────────────────────────────
    96 // grsai 响应格式: {"id":"..."}{"status":"running"}{"status":"succeeded","results":[...]}
    97 // 标准 JSON.parse 会在这种格式上失败，需要按花括号深度逐段切割
    98 function parseStreamingJson(raw: string): GrsaiChunk[] {
    99   const cleaned = raw.replace(/^\uFEFF/, '').trim();
   100   if (!cleaned) return [];
   101 
   102   // 检测 HTML 错误页（网关/CDN 返回）
   103   if (cleaned.startsWith('<!') || cleaned.toLowerCase().startsWith('<html')) {
   104     const title = cleaned.match(/<title[^>]*>(.*?)<\/title>/i)?.[1] || '';
   105     throw new Error(`服务返回 HTML 错误页${title ? `: ${title}` : ''}，请检查 API 地址`);
   106   }
   107 
   108   const chunks: GrsaiChunk[] = [];
   109   let depth = 0;
   110   let start = -1;
   111   let inString = false;
   112   let escape = false;
   113 
   114   for (let i = 0; i < cleaned.length; i++) {
   115     const ch = cleaned[i];
   116 
   117     // 字符串内转义处理
   118     if (escape) { escape = false; continue; }
   119     if (ch === '\\' && inString) { escape = true; continue; }
   120     if (ch === '"') { inString = !inString; continue; }
   121     if (inString) continue;
   122 
   123     if (ch === '{') {
   124       if (depth === 0) start = i;
   125       depth++;
   126     } else if (ch === '}') {
   127       depth--;
   128       if (depth === 0 && start !== -1) {
   129         const fragment = cleaned.slice(start, i + 1);
   130         try {
   131           chunks.push(JSON.parse(fragment) as GrsaiChunk);
   132         } catch {
   133           console.warn(`[generate-image] 跳过无效片段: ${fragment.slice(0, 80)}`);
   134         }
   135         start = -1;
   136       }
   137     }
   138   }
   139 
   140   return chunks;
   141 }
   142 
   143 // ─── 从最终 chunk 中判断是否成功并提取图片 URL ────────────────────────────────
   144 
   145 // 宽松的成功判断：兼容 grsai 所有可能的 status/code 字段
   146 function isSuccessChunk(chunk: GrsaiChunk): boolean {
   147   // status 字符串全覆盖
   148   const status = String(chunk.status ?? '').toLowerCase();
   149   if (['succeeded', 'success', 'done', 'complete', 'completed', 'finished', 'ok', '200'].includes(status)) return true;
   150 
   151   // 数字/字符串 code：0 或 200 视为成功
   152   const code = chunk.code;
   153   if (code === 0 || code === '0' || code === 200 || code === '200') return true;
   154 
   155   // progress >= 100
   156   if (typeof chunk.progress === 'number' && chunk.progress >= 100) return true;
   157 
   158   // 含图片数据的数组字段（只要非空就算成功）
   159   if (Array.isArray(chunk.results) && chunk.results.length > 0) return true;
   160   if (Array.isArray(chunk.data)    && chunk.data.length > 0)    return true;
   161   if (Array.isArray(chunk.images)  && chunk.images.length > 0)  return true;
   162   if (Array.isArray(chunk.output)  && chunk.output.length > 0)  return true;
   163 
   164   // 顶层直接有 URL
   165   if (typeof chunk.url === 'string' && chunk.url.startsWith('http')) return true;
   166 
   167   return false;
   168 }
   169 
   170 // 递归深度扫描：找到任意一个 http(s) URL 字符串
   171 function deepFindUrl(obj: unknown, depth = 0): string | undefined {
   172   if (depth > 6) return undefined;
   173   if (typeof obj === 'string') {
   174     return (obj.startsWith('http://') || obj.startsWith('https://')) ? obj : undefined;
   175   }
   176   if (Array.isArray(obj)) {
   177     for (const item of obj) {
   178       const found = deepFindUrl(item, depth + 1);
   179       if (found) return found;
   180     }
   181   }
   182   if (obj && typeof obj === 'object') {
   183     // 优先检查高概率字段
   184     const priorityKeys = ['url', 'uri', 'image_url', 'imageUrl', 'src', 'link'];
   185     const rec = obj as Record<string, unknown>;
   186     for (const k of priorityKeys) {
   187       const found = deepFindUrl(rec[k], depth + 1);
   188       if (found) return found;
   189     }
   190     // 再扫描其余字段
   191     for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(rec)) {
   192       if (priorityKeys.includes(k)) continue;
   193       const found = deepFindUrl(v, depth + 1);
   194       if (found) return found;
   195     }
   196   }
   197   return undefined;
   198 }
   199 
   200 function extractImageUrl(chunk: GrsaiChunk): string | undefined {
   201   // grsai 格式：results[0].url 或 results[0].uri
   202   if (Array.isArray(chunk.results) && chunk.results.length > 0) {
   203     return chunk.results[0].url || chunk.results[0].uri;
   204   }
   205   // OpenAI 标准：data[0].url
   206   if (Array.isArray(chunk.data) && chunk.data.length > 0) {
   207     return (chunk.data as ImageItem[])[0]?.url;
   208   }
   209   // 其他兼容格式
   210   if (Array.isArray(chunk.images) && chunk.images.length > 0) return chunk.images[0].url;
   211   if (Array.isArray(chunk.output) && chunk.output.length > 0) return (chunk.output[0] as ImageItem).url;
   212   if (typeof chunk.url === 'string' && chunk.url.startsWith('http')) return chunk.url;
   213   return undefined;
   214 }
   215 
   216 function extractB64(chunk: GrsaiChunk): string | undefined {
   217   if (Array.isArray(chunk.results) && chunk.results.length > 0) return chunk.results[0].b64_json;
   218   if (Array.isArray(chunk.data) && chunk.data.length > 0) return (chunk.data as ImageItem[])[0]?.b64_json;
   219   if (typeof chunk.b64_json === 'string' && chunk.b64_json) return chunk.b64_json;
   220   return undefined;
   221 }
   222 
   223 // ─── 将英文 API 错误翻译为用户友好的中文提示 ──────────────────────────────────
   224 function friendlyErrorMessage(raw: string): string {
   225   const s = raw.toLowerCase();
   226   if (s.includes('insufficient credits') || s.includes('insufficient balance') ||
   227       s.includes('quota exceeded') || s.includes('rate limit') ||
   228       s.includes('billing') || s.includes('credit')) {
   229     return `API 余额不足，请前往 grsai 平台为账户充值后重试（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   230   }
   231   if (s.includes('invalid api key') || s.includes('unauthorized') ||
   232       s.includes('authentication') || s.includes('api key')) {
   233     return `API Key 无效或已过期，请在设置页面重新配置（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   234   }
   235   if (s.includes('content policy') || s.includes('safety') ||
   236       s.includes('violated') || s.includes('blocked')) {
   237     return `提示词触发内容安全限制，请修改描述后重试（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   238   }
   239   if (s.includes('timeout') || s.includes('timed out')) {
   240     return `请求超时，请稍后重试（原始信息：${raw}）`;
   241   }
   242   return raw;
   243 }
   244 
   245 // ─── 从错误 chunk 中提取可读信息 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   246 function extractErrorMessage(chunk: GrsaiChunk, httpStatus: number): string {
   247   let raw = '';
   248   if (chunk.error) {
   249     if (typeof chunk.error === 'object') {
   250       raw = chunk.error.message || chunk.error.msg || JSON.stringify(chunk.error);
   251     } else if (typeof chunk.error === 'string') {
   252       raw = chunk.error;
   253     }
   254   }
   255   if (!raw && typeof chunk.message === 'string') raw = chunk.message;
   256   if (!raw && typeof chunk.msg    === 'string') raw = chunk.msg;
   257   if (!raw && typeof chunk.detail === 'string') raw = chunk.detail;
   258   if (!raw) return `API 请求失败 (HTTP ${httpStatus})`;
   259   return friendlyErrorMessage(raw);
   260 }
   261 
   262 // ─── Edge Function 入口 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   263 serve(async (req: Request) => {
   264   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
   265     return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });
   266   }
   267 
   268   const jsonResp = (body: unknown, status = 200) =>
   269     new Response(JSON.stringify(body), {
   270       status,
   271       headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   272     });
   273 
   274   try {
   275     let body: Record<string, unknown>;
   276     try {
   277       body = await req.json();
   278     } catch {
   279       // fallback：部分代理转发时 Content-Type 可能不匹配，尝试手动解析文本
   280       try {
   281         const text = await req.text();
   282         body = JSON.parse(text);
   283       } catch {
   284         return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请求体 JSON 格式错误' }, 400);
   285       }
   286     }
   287 
   288     // 优先从 body 读取凭证（秒哒代理会剥离自定义 header），兼容旧版 header 传参
   289     const apiKey =
   290       (body.apiKey as string | undefined) ||
   291       req.headers.get('x-api-key') ||
   292       '';
   293     if (!apiKey) {
   294       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '未提供 API Key，请在设置页面配置' }, 401);
   295     }
   296 
   297     const baseUrl =
   298       (body.baseUrl as string | undefined) ||
   299       req.headers.get('x-base-url') ||
   300       DEFAULT_ENDPOINT;
   301     const modelName =
   302       (body.modelName as string | undefined) ||
   303       req.headers.get('x-model-name') ||
   304       'gpt-image-2';
   305 
   306     const {
   307       prompt,
   308       size = '1:1',
   309       n = 1,
   310       variants = 1,
   311       response_format = 'url',
   312     } = body as {
   313       prompt?: string;
   314       size?: string;
   315       n?: number;
   316       variants?: number;
   317       response_format?: string;
   318     };
   319 
   320     if (!prompt?.trim()) {
   321       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '请输入图片描述' }, 400);
   322     }
   323 
   324     // GrsAI gpt-image-2：size 使用比例格式，参数名为 variants，移除 style 等不支持字段
   325     const requestPayload = {
   326       model: modelName,
   327       prompt: prompt.trim(),
   328       variants: Number(variants) || Number(n) || 1,
   329       size: pixelSizeToRatio(String(size)),
   330       response_format: String(response_format),
   331     };
   332 
   333     console.log(`[generate-image] endpoint=${baseUrl} model=${modelName} size=${size}`);
   334     console.log(`[generate-image] prompt=${String(prompt).slice(0, 80)}`);
   335 
   336     // ── 发起请求 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   337     let response: Response;
   338     try {
   339       response = await fetchWithRetry(
   340         baseUrl,
   341         {
   342           method: 'POST',
   343           headers: {
   344             'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   345             'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   346           },
   347           body: JSON.stringify(requestPayload),
   348         },
   349         MAX_RETRIES,
   350         REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS,
   351       );
   352     } catch (err) {
   353       const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   354       console.error(`[generate-image] 所有重试失败: ${msg}`);

   360 
   361     // ── 解析流式 JSON 响应 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   362     let chunks: GrsaiChunk[];
   363     try {

   365     } catch (parseErr) {
   366       const msg = parseErr instanceof Error ? parseErr.message : String(parseErr);
   367       console.error(`[generate-image] 响应解析失败: ${msg}`);
   368       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: msg }, 502);
   369     }
   370 
   371     console.log(`[generate-image] 解析得到 ${chunks.length} 个 JSON 片段`);
   372 
   373     if (chunks.length === 0) {
   374       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: '服务返回空响应，请稍后重试' }, 502);
   375     }
   376

   378     if (!response.ok) {
   379       const errMsg = extractErrorMessage(chunks[0], response.status);

   381       return jsonResp({ success: false, error: errMsg }, response.status);
   382     }
   383 
   384     // ── 取最后一个 chunk 作为最终结果 ──────────────────────────────────────────

   389     const successChunk = isSuccessChunk(lastChunk)
   390       ? lastChunk
   391       : [...chunks].reverse().find(isSuccessChunk);
